    <div style="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><p style="margin: 0pt">&#160;</p></div>

<p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&#160;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<td style="width: 1in; text-align: left"><b><span style="text-decoration: underline">Item 3.02</span></b></td><td style="text-align: justify"><b><span style="text-decoration: underline">Unregistered Sales of Equity
                                            Securities.</span></b></td>
</tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">As previously reported, on April&#160;6, 2022,
Rockwell Medical,&#160;Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) and DaVita Inc. (&#8220;DaVita&#8221;) entered into a Securities Purchase Agreement,
pursuant to which the Company agreed to issue up to $15 million of preferred stock to DaVita. The Company initially issued 7,500 shares
of a newly designated series of preferred stock, which was designated &#8220;Series&#160;X Convertible Preferred Stock&#8221; (the &#8220;Series&#160;X
Preferred Stock&#8221;) for gross proceeds of $7,500,000 in connection therewith.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">On June&#160;16, 2022, following the achievement
of a capital raise milestone by the Company, the Company issued an additional 7,500 shares of Series&#160;X Preferred Stock to DaVita
in a second closing for gross proceeds of $7,500,000. The offering and sale of the Series&#160;X Preferred Stock was exempt from registration
under Section&#160;4(a)(2)&#160;of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<td style="width: 1in; text-align: left"><b><span style="text-decoration: underline">Item 5.02</span></b></td><td style="text-align: justify"><b><span style="text-decoration: underline">Departure of Directors
                                            or Principal Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Principal Officers.</span></b></td>
</tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><i>Departure of President and Chief Executive Officer
and Director</i></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">On June&#160;22, 2022, the Company announced that Russell H. Ellison, M.D., M.Sc., will be stepping down from his role as the President and Chief
Executive Officer of the Company, effective as of June&#160;30, 2022 (the &#8220;separation date&#8221;). Effective as of the separation
date, Dr.&#160;Ellison will also resign from the board of directors of the Company (the &#8220;Board&#8221;).</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">Pursuant to his employment agreement, subject to
Dr.&#160;Ellison&#8217;s execution and non-revocation of a release agreement in favor of the Company and continued compliance with certain
restrictive covenants, including covenants relating to confidentiality, non-interference, non-competition and non-solicitation, Dr.&#160;Ellison
will receive the following payments and benefits: (i)&#160;an amount equal to the sum of (A)&#160;$500,000, representing Dr.&#160;Ellison&#8217;s
annualized base salary; and (B)&#160;$350,000, representing 100% of Dr.&#160;Ellison&#8217;s annual target bonus, payable in equal installments
and in accordance with the Company&#8217;s regular payroll schedule for a period of 12 months following the separation date, (ii)&#160;reimbursement
of Dr.&#160;Ellison&#8217;s costs for medical coverage for up to one year (or, if sooner, until he receives substantially similar coverage
from another employer), and (iii)&#160;the time-based stock options granted to Dr.&#160;Ellison in connection with his commencement of
employment will continue to vest for a period of one year and all stock options held by Dr.&#160;Ellison that are exercisable as of the
separation date and all stock options that become exercisable over the one-year period following the separation date will remain exercisable
until the one-year anniversary of the separation date.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><i>Appointment of President and Chief Executive
Officer</i></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">On June&#160;21, 2022, the Board appointed Mark
Strobeck, Ph.D. as the Company&#8217;s President and Chief Executive Officer and as a Class&#160;III Director to serve until the Company&#8217;s
2024 Annual Meeting of Stockholders and until his successor is duly elected and qualified, effective July&#160;1, 2022.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">Dr.&#160;Strobeck, age 51, has held leadership
positions in both emerging biotechnology and pharmaceutical companies for more than twenty years. Most recently, he served as Managing
Director of Aquilo Partners, LP, a life sciences investment bank, from May&#160;2021 to June&#160;2022. He previously served as Executive
Vice President and Chief Operating Officer of Assertio Holdings,&#160;Inc., a pharmaceutical company, from May&#160;2020 to December&#160;2020.
Prior to that, Dr.&#160;Strobeck was Executive Vice President and Chief Operating Officer of Zyla Life Sciences, a pharmaceutical company,
from September&#160;2015 through its merger with Assertio Holdings,&#160;Inc. in May&#160;2020, and previously served as Zyla&#8217;s
Chief Business Officer from January&#160;2014 to September&#160;2015. Before his employment at Zyla, he served as Zyla&#8217;s advisor
from June&#160;2012 to December&#160;2013. From January&#160;2012 to December&#160;2013, he served as President and Chief Executive Officer
and a director of Corridor Pharmaceuticals,&#160;Inc., a pharmaceuticals company, which was acquired by AstraZeneca plc in 2014. From
December&#160;2010 to October&#160;2011, Dr.&#160;Strobeck served as Chief Business Officer of Topaz Pharmaceuticals Inc., a specialty
pharmaceutical company acquired by Sanofi Pasteur in the fourth quarter of 2011. From June&#160;2010 to November&#160;2010 and October&#160;2011
to January&#160;2012, Dr.&#160;Strobeck worked as a consultant. From January&#160;2008 to May&#160;2010, Dr.&#160;Strobeck served as Chief
Business Officer of Trevena,&#160;Inc., a pharmaceutical company. Prior to joining Trevena, Dr.&#160;Strobeck held management roles at
GlaxoSmithKline plc, a pharmaceuticals company, and venture capital firms SR One Limited and EuclidSR Partners, L.P. Dr.&#160;Strobeck
currently serves on the board of directors of Horse Power For Life, a nonprofit organization dedicated to improving the quality of life
for individuals diagnosed with cancer, a position he has held since 2012. Dr.&#160;Strobeck received his B.S. in Biology from St. Lawrence
University and his Ph.D. in Pharmacology and Biophysics from the University of Cincinnati, and completed his post-doctoral fellowship
at the University of Pennsylvania. There is no information that is required to be disclosed with respect to Dr.&#160;Strobeck pursuant
to Item 404(a)&#160;of Regulation S-K.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></p>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2 -->
    <div style="border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><p style="margin: 0pt">&#160;</p></div>
    <div style="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><p style="margin: 0pt">&#160;</p></div>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">On June&#160;21, 2022, in connection with Dr.&#160;Strobeck&#8217;s
commencement of employment, the Company entered into an employment agreement with Dr.&#160;Strobeck pursuant to which he will serve as
the Company&#8217;s President and Chief Executive Officer (the &#8220;Employment Agreement&#8221;). The Employment Agreement provides
that Dr.&#160;Strobeck will serve as an at-will employee. Dr.&#160;Strobeck will receive an annualized base salary of $550,000 (&#8220;Base
Salary&#8221;). He will be eligible to earn year-end performance bonuses with a target bonus opportunity of 60% of his Base Salary (&#8220;Target
Bonus&#8221;) and is eligible to participate in the employee benefit plans and programs generally available to the Company&#8217;s similarly
situated senior executives. Dr.&#160;Strobeck is also eligible to receive annual long-term incentive grants consistent with similar practices
for the Company&#8217;s senior executives, awarded at the discretion of the Compensation Committee of the Board. In connection with his
commencement of employment, he received an initial equity grant comprised of a time-based option to purchase up to 400,000 shares of the
Company&#8217;s common stock (the &#8220;Initial Time-Based Options&#8221;).</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">Under the Employment Agreement, upon a termination
of Dr.&#160;Strobeck&#8217;s employment due to death or Disability, any equity awards held by Dr.&#160;Strobeck subject to time-based
vesting conditions will accelerate and become fully vested. All stock options held by Dr.&#160;Strobeck that are exercisable as of the
date of such termination, including any stock options that accelerate in connection with such termination, will remain exercisable until
the earlier of one year following such termination and the expiration date of the stock options.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">Under the Employment Agreement, upon a termination
of Dr.&#160;Strobeck&#8217;s employment by the Company without Cause or by Dr.&#160;Strobeck for Good Reason, Dr.&#160;Strobeck will be
entitled to receive, subject to his execution and non-revocation of a separation agreement and release of claims in favor of the Company
and compliance with certain restrictive covenants, (i)&#160;an amount equal to his Base Salary then in effect, payable in equal installments
for a one-year period, (ii)&#160;a pro-rated bonus for the year of termination, based on achievement of actual performance for the full
performance period and pro-rated based on the portion of the performance period Dr.&#160;Strobeck was employed prior to termination, payable
in a lump sum after the completion of the full performance, (iii)&#160;reimbursement of COBRA coverage for up to one year (or, if sooner,
until he receives substantially similar coverage from another employer), and (iv)&#160;Dr.&#160;Strobeck&#8217;s Initial Time-Based Options
will continue to vest for a period of one year and all stock options held by Dr.&#160;Strobeck that are exercisable as of the date of
such termination and all stock options that become exercisable over the one-year period following such termination, will remain exercisable
until the earlier of one year following such termination and the expiration date of the stock options.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">Under the Employment Agreement, in the event of
a Change of Control, upon a termination of Dr.&#160;Strobeck&#8217;s employment by the Company without Cause or by Executive for Good
Reason during the Effective Period, subject to his compliance with certain restrictive covenants, Dr.&#160;Strobeck will be entitled to
receive (i)&#160;an amount equal to the sum of (A)&#160;1.5 times his Base Salary then in effect plus (B)&#160;100% of his annual Target
Bonus, (ii)&#160;reimbursement of COBRA coverage for up to two years (or, if sooner, until he receives substantially similar coverage
from another employer or is no longer eligible for COBRA coverage) and (iii)&#160;any equity awards held by Dr.&#160;Strobeck subject
to time-based vesting conditions will accelerate and become fully vested and all stock options held by Dr.&#160;Strobeck that are exercisable
as of the date of such termination, including any stock options that accelerate in connection with such termination, will remain exercisable
until the expiration date of the stock options.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">In connection with the Employment Agreement, Dr.&#160;Strobeck
also entered into the Company&#8217;s form of Employee Confidentiality, Assignment of Inventions, Non-Interference and Non-Competition
Agreement.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">Capitalized terms used in herein, but not defined,
shall have the meanings given to them in the Employment Agreement. The foregoing summary of the Employment Agreement does not purport
to be a complete description of the Employment Agreement and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the full text of the Employment
Agreement, which the Company intends to file with its quarterly report on Form&#160;10-Q for the quarter ended June&#160;30, 2022.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top">

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">On June&#160;22, 2022, the Company issued a press
release announcing the appointment of Dr.&#160;Strobeck as President and Chief Executive Officer and director. Attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;99.1
and incorporated herein by reference, is a copy of the press release.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">In accordance with General Instruction B.2 of Form&#160;8-K,

statement or other document filed under the Securities Act or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference
in such filing.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Rockwell Medical,&nbsp;Inc. Appoints Mark Strobeck,
Ph.D., as President and Chief Executive Officer</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>WIXOM, Mich., June&nbsp;22, 2022 </B>-- <U>Rockwell
Medical</U>,&nbsp;Inc. (Nasdaq: RMTI), a biopharmaceutical company dedicated to transforming the treatment of iron deficiency and anemia
management, today announced that the Board of Directors has appointed Mark Strobeck, Ph.D., as President and Chief Executive Officer,
effective July&nbsp;1, 2022. Dr.&nbsp;Strobeck will also join the Company&rsquo;s Board of Directors. Russell Ellison, M.D., M.Sc<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">.,
</FONT>will be stepping down as President and Chief Executive Officer and as a member of the Company&rsquo;s Board of Directors effective
June&nbsp;30, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&ldquo;We are excited to have Mark join Rockwell
as our new President and Chief Executive Officer&rdquo; said Robert S. Radie, Chairman of the Board of Directors of Rockwell Medical.
 &ldquo;Mark&rsquo;s scientific, operational, and business experience along with his successful track record align well with Rockwell&rsquo;s
goal to develop and commercialize transformative treatments for iron deficiency in multiple disease states. On behalf of the Board of
Directors, we thank Dr.&nbsp;Russell Ellison for his contributions to Rockwell over the last 2 years and wish him well in the future.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&ldquo;I am incredibly excited to join Rockwell
and grateful for the support of Rockwell&rsquo;s Board in entrusting me to lead the next phase of Rockwell&rsquo;s development,&rdquo;
said Dr.&nbsp;Strobeck. &ldquo;I am impressed with Rockwell&rsquo;s proprietary drug technology and excited to drive forward its development
toward the potential treatment of iron deficiency in the home infusion setting, and longer term in acute heart failure. Additionally,
as one of the largest suppliers of life saving concentrates for dialysis patients in the U.S., Rockwell has a unique opportunity, working
with distributors and customers, to grow and develop this critical business. The company has made significant progress and I look forward
to working with Rockwell&rsquo;s Board of Directors and the talented Rockwell team to build upon this momentum.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">Mark Strobeck, Ph.D.
brings 20+ years of operating, business development, capital raising and investing experience in life sciences for both private and public
biotechnology companies. Prior to joining Rockwell Medical, Mark was a Managing Partner at Aquilo Partners, a life science investment
banking firm specializing in mergers and acquisitions and strategic partnering transactions. Mark was Chief Operating Officer at Zyla
Lifesciences (acquired by Assertio Therapeutics), President and CEO of Corridor Pharmaceuticals (acquired by AstraZeneca), and Chief
Business Officer of Topaz Pharmaceuticals (acquired by Sanofi Pasteur). He also served as Chief Business Officer of Trevena,&nbsp;Inc.
and Vice President of Business Development at GlaxoSmithKline (GSK) where he was responsible for numerous transactions including GSK&rsquo;s
+$1B agreement with Chemocentryx. Earlier in his career, he worked at two venture capital firms, SR One (GSK&rsquo;s formally wholly
owned venture capital firm) and EuclidSR Partners making investments in drug discovery and drug development companies.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">Mark received a doctorate
in biophysics and pharmacology from the University of Cincinnati and completed his post-doctoral fellowship at the University of Pennsylvania.
He also received a BS from St. Lawrence University.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 33%">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 34%; text-align: center">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 33%; text-align: right">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Notice of Issuance of Inducement Grants</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Rockwell also announced the grant of an inducement
award to Dr.&nbsp;Strobeck as an inducement material to Dr.&nbsp;Strobeck&rsquo;s employment pursuant to Rule&nbsp;5635(c)(4)&nbsp;of
the Nasdaq Listing Rules. In connection with his commencement of employment, Dr.&nbsp;Strobeck was granted an inducement award consisting
of a stock option to purchase up to 400,000 shares of Rockwell common stock, which vests 25% on the first four anniversaries of the grant
date. The exercise price of the stock option will equal the closing price of the Company&rsquo;s common stock on July&nbsp;1, 2022, the
date of the grant.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>About Rockwell Medical</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Rockwell Medical<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">&nbsp;is
a commercial-stage biopharmaceutical company developing and commercializing its next-generation parenteral iron technology platform,
Ferric Pyrophosphate Citrate (FPC), which has the potential to lead transformative treatments for iron deficiency in multiple disease
states, reduce healthcare costs and improve patients' lives. The Company has two FDA-approved therapies indicated for patients undergoing
hemodialysis, which are the first two products developed from the FPC platform.&nbsp;</FONT>Rockwell Medical<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">&nbsp;is
also advancing its FPC platform by developing FPC for the treatment of iron deficiency anemia in patients outside of dialysis, who are
receiving intravenous medications in the home infusion setting. In addition,&nbsp;</FONT>Rockwell Medical<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">&nbsp;is
one of two major suppliers of life-saving hemodialysis concentrate products to kidney dialysis clinics in&nbsp;</FONT>the United States<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">.
For more information, visit&nbsp;<U>www.RockwellMed.com</U>.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>
